	id = brazil_adhemar.1
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar.1"
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar.1.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_adhemar_6

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = brazil_adhemar.1.a
		add_political_power = 20
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_adhemar.7
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar.7"
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar.7.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar.7.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_trade_discussion

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar.7.a
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.02 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.05 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		TNO_improve_health_care_policy_effectiveness_low = yes
	}

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar.7.b
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.06 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_modifier = 10 }
		USA = {
			add_to_trade_modifier_PREV = yes
		}
		TNO_improve_health_care_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
		set_temp_variable = { slush_amount = 0.5 }
		BRA_adhemar_add_slush_fund = yes
	}

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar.7.c
		set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.06 }
		econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_modifier = 10 }

			add_to_trade_modifier_PREV = yes
		}
		TNO_improve_health_care_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
		set_temp_variable = { slush_amount = 0.5 }

	}

			limit = {

		}
		else = {
			BRA_boost_PSP_candidates_northeast_med = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = brazil_adhemar.29.c

			}
			BRA_adhemaredna_decrease_cooperation_low = yes
			BRA_adhemaredna_regular_increase_edna_influence = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { ## Itaipu Negotiations event chain
	id = brazil_adhemar.128
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar.128"
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar.128.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar.128.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_adhemar_10

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar.128.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAR = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Federico_Chaves
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Juan_Natalicio_Gonzalez
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Edgar_Ynsfran
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Victoriano_Benitez_Vera
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Epifanio_Mendez_Fleitas
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.129
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PAR_OAS_victory
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.130
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAR = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.131
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAR = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = PAR_Alfredo_Stroessner
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.132
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				PAR = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Rafael_Franco
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Alfredo_Ramos
							ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_country_leader = {
							character = PAR_Gustavo_Gonzalez
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.133
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { ## Total Success event: Paraguay enters Brazilian sphere
	id = brazil_adhemar.149
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar.149"
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar.149.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar.149.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_adhemar_6

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar.149.a
		if = {
			limit = { PAR = { check_variable = { ECON_SPHERE_LEADER = ARG } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_Adhemar_Paraguay_enters_sphere_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_Adhemar_Paraguay_enters_sphere_tooltip_2
		}
		BRA_adhemaredna_regular_increase_adhemar_influence = yes
		set_country_flag = BRA_paraguyan_negotiations_success
		set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 1 }
		econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
		PAR = {
			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 1 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = BRA
				modifier = BRA_itaipu_dam
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { ECON_SPHERE_LEADER = BRA } } }
				econ_leave_sphere = yes
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.UNALIGNED = 60 }
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.ARGENTINA = 40 }
				SA_set_alignment = yes
				STC = {
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.BRAZIL = 10 }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.UNALIGNED = 60 }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.ARGENTINA = 30 }
					SA_set_alignment = yes
					econ_leave_sphere = yes
				}
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PAR
			modifier = BRA_itaipu_dam
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_adhemar.1000
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar.1000"
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar.1000.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar.1000.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_brasilia_1

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar.1000.a
		BRA_boost_PSP_candidates_nationwide_med = yes
		set_temp_variable = { temp_law = token:BRA_healthcare_bill_adhemar_law }
		TNO_add_assorted_law = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = BRA_shut_her_out
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = tno_health_care_support_for_emergencies_dummy
					add_idea = tno_health_care_low_income_protections_dummy
				}
			}
			TNO_improve_health_care_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = tno_health_care_support_for_emergencies
					add_idea = tno_health_care_low_income_protections
				}
				TNO_improve_health_care_policy_effectiveness_high = yes
				country_event = brazil_adhemar.179
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar.158 days = 365 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = BRA_let_her_in
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = tno_health_care_support_for_emergencies_dummy
					add_idea = tno_health_care_free_universal_care_dummy
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_megaproject_sus_effect
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = tno_health_care_support_for_emergencies
					add_idea = tno_health_care_free_universal_care
				}
				BRA_start_sus_healthcare_project = yes
				country_event = brazil_adhemar.178
				country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar.157 days = 365 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_adhemar.1008
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar.1008"
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar.1008.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar.1008.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_trade_discussion

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = brazil_adhemar.1008.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS
						option = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS_TANCREDO
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS
							option = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS_VARGAS
						}
						check_variable = {
							neves_brizola_influence > 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		add_to_variable = {
			var = neves_brizola_influence
			value = 1
			tooltip = BRA_neves_influence
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						neves_brizola_influence > 0
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.1009
					days = 35
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						neves_brizola_influence < 0
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.1010
					days = 35
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.1011
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = brazil_adhemar.1008.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS
						option = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS_BRIZOLA
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS
							option = BRA_1970_ELECTIONS_VARGAS
						}
						check_variable = {
							neves_brizola_influence < 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = neves_brizola_influence
			value = 1
			tooltip = BRA_brizola_influence
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						neves_brizola_influence > 0
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.1009
					days = 35
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						neves_brizola_influence < 0
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.1010
					days = 35
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = brazil_adhemar.1011
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = brazil_adhemar_coma.2901
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar_coma.2901"
		set_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_fate_decided
	}
	title = brazil_adhemar_coma.2901.t
	desc = brazil_adhemar_coma.2901.desc
	hidden = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_adhemar_10

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar_coma.2901.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE
							option = DEFAULT
						}
						AND = {
							has_game_rule = {
								rule = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE
								option = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE_DIES
							}
							OR = {
								has_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_won_the_100_days
								has_country_flag = GER_Espionage_operation_schild_flag_2
							}
						}
					}
					check_variable = {
						BRA_adhemar_coma_trigger > 2
					}
				}
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE
					option = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE_SURVIVES
				}

			}
		}
		country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.30 days = 10 }
	}

	option = { #
		name = brazil_adhemar_coma.2901.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						BRA_adhemar_coma_trigger < 3
					}
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_Espionage_operation_schild_flag_2 }
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE
						option = DEFAULT
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE
						option = BRA_ADHEMAR_FATE_DIES
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_won_the_100_days
						has_country_flag = GER_Espionage_operation_schild_flag_2
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.31 days = 10 }
	}
}

country_event = { # America - Adhemar Death
	id = brazil_adhemar_assassination.7
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event brazil_adhemar_assassination.7"
	}

	desc = brazil_adhemar_assassination.7.desc

	option = {
		name = brazil_adhemar_assassination.7.a
		set_country_flag = USA_killed_adhemar
		hidden_effect = {
			BRA = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = BRA_Edna_Lott_hog }
					country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.45 days = 5 }
					country_event = { id = brazil_adhemar_coma.46 days = 10 }
					load_focus_tree = { tree = BRA_Adhemar_return_to_normality keep_completed = yes }
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
					BRA_give_up_on_bill = yes
					remove_all_ministers = yes
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_country_flag = BRA_Edna_UDN_compromise
						}
						add_ideas = { BRA_Pedro_Aleixo_hog BRA_Vasco_Leitao_da_Cunha_adhemar_for BRA_Ignacio_Rangel_eco BRA_Alfeu_de_Alcantara_Monteiro_sec }
					}
					else = {
						add_ideas = { BRA_Pedro_Aleixo_hog BRA_Evandro_Lins_e_Silva_for BRA_Romeu_de_Campos_Vergal_edna_eco BRA_Alfeu_de_Alcantara_Monteiro_sec }
					}
					clr_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_moneybags_category_allowed
					clr_country_flag = BRA_adhemaredna_category_allowed
					promote_character = {
						character = BRA_Edna_Lott
						ideology = progressivism_subtype
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = progressivism
					}
					set_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_killed
				}
				else = {
					promote_character = {
						character = BRA_Pedro_Aleixo
						ideology = paternalism_right_wing_populism_subtype
					}
					load_focus_tree = { tree = BRA_Adhemar_adhemar_gone keep_completed = yes }
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
					BRA_give_up_on_bill = yes
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { id = LATAM_news.267 hours = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}
